    var elem = document.getElementById("mc-subscribe-form");
    elem.parentElement.removeChild(elem);
    
    function checkInlineInputs() {
      var re = /^((([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+(\.([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+)*)|((\x22)((((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(([\x01-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f\x7f]|\x21|[\x23-\x5b]|[\x5d-\x7e]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(\\([\x01-\x09\x0b\x0c\x0d-\x7f]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF]))))*(((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(\x22)))@((([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])))\.)+(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF]))){2,6}$/i;
      var validated = true;
      if(document.querySelector("#inline-email").value == "") {
        document.querySelector("#inline-email").classList.add('validation-failed');
        document.querySelector("#inline-email").focus();
        return false;
      }
      else if(!re.test(document.querySelector("#inline-email").value)) {
        document.querySelector("#inline-email").classList.add('validation-failed');
        document.querySelector("#inline-email").focus();
        return false;
      }
      else if(!document.querySelector('#inline_newsletter_agreement').checked) {
      	alert(document.querySelector('#inline_newsletter_agreement').getAttribute("data-validation-err"));
        return false;
   	  }
      document.querySelector("#inline-email").classList.remove('validation-failed');
      return true;
    }
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
      $("body").on("submit", "#webchannel-inline-form", function() {
      	if(checkInlineInputs()) {
          	$.showLoadingSpinner();
          	setTimeout(function() {
              $("#inline_newsletter_agreement").prop("checked", false);
              $("#inline-email").val("");
              $.hideLoadingSpinner();
              setTimeout(function() {
              	alert("Tack fr att du anmlt dig till vrt nyhetsbrev!");
              }, 500);
            }, 1500);
        	
        }
      });
    });

function shareFavorites(shareurl, imageurl, description) {
    $("ajax-loading-overlay").show();
     FB.ui(
            {
              method: 'feed',
              name: 'Mina delade favoriter',
              link: shareurl,
              picture: imageurl,
              caption: '',
              description: description
            },
            function(response) {
                $("ajax-loading-overlay").hide();
               var posted, msg;
              if (response && response.post_id) {
                posted = true;
              } else {
                posted = false;
              }
              if(posted) {
                    $("share-response-message").addClassName("green");
                    msg = "Inlgget har publicerats";
                }
                else {
                    $("share-response-message").addClassName("red");
                    msg = "Inlgget publicerades inte";
                }
                $("share-response-message").update(msg).show();
                $("terms-overlay").select(".share-wrapper")[0].setStyle({height: "420px"});
            }
          );
}

function shareProduct(shareurl, imageurl, productName, description) {
    $("ajax-loading-overlay").show();
     FB.ui(
            {
              method: 'share',
              href: shareurl
            },
            function(response) {
                $("ajax-loading-overlay").hide();
               var posted, msg;
              if (response && !response.error_code) {
                posted = true;
              } else {
                posted = false;
              }
              if(posted) {
                    
                    msg = "Inlgget har publicerats";
                }
                else {
                    
                    msg = "Inlgget publicerades inte";
                }
                
                alert(msg);
            }
          );
}

function sharePost(shareurl, imageurl, postTitle) {
    $("ajax-loading-overlay").show();
     FB.ui(
            {
              method: 'share',
              link: shareurl
            },
            function(response) {
                $("ajax-loading-overlay").hide();
               var posted, msg;
              if (response && !response.error_code) {
                posted = true;
              } else {
                posted = false;
              }
              if(posted) {
                    
                    msg = "Inlgget har publicerats";
                }
                else {
                    
                    msg = "Inlgget publicerades inte";
                }
                
                alert(msg);
            }
          );
}

<script language="javascript">
              	
                function checkInputs() {
                    var re = /^((([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+(\.([a-z]|\d|[!#\$%&'\*\+\-\/=\?\^_`{\|}~]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])+)*)|((\x22)((((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(([\x01-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f\x7f]|\x21|[\x23-\x5b]|[\x5d-\x7e]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(\\([\x01-\x09\x0b\x0c\x0d-\x7f]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF]))))*(((\x20|\x09)*(\x0d\x0a))?(\x20|\x09)+)?(\x22)))@((([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|\d|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])))\.)+(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])|(([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])([a-z]|\d|-|\.|_|~|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF])*([a-z]|[\u00A0-\uD7FF\uF900-\uFDCF\uFDF0-\uFFEF]))){2,6}$/i;
                    var validated = true;
                    
                    if(document.querySelector("#webchannel-email").value == "") {
                        validated = false;
                    }
                    else if(!re.test(document.querySelector("#webchannel-email").value)) {
                        validated = false;
                    }
                    if (!validated) {
                        document.querySelector("#webchannel-email-wrapper").classList.add('validation-failed');
                        document.querySelector("#webchannel-email").classList.add('validation-failed');
                        document.querySelector("#webchannel-email").focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                    else {
                        document.querySelector("#webchannel-email-wrapper").classList.remove('validation-failed');
                        document.querySelector("#webchannel-email").classList.remove('validation-failed');
                    }
                    
                    return validated;
                }
                jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
                    $("#webchannel-email").attr("value", $("#webchannel-email").val());
                    $("body").on("focusin", ".inputbox-v2", function () {
                        $(".inputbox-v2").removeClass("hilight");
                        $(this).addClass('hilight');
                    }).on("click", ".inputbox-v2", function () {
                        $(this).find('input').focus();
                    }).on("blur", ".inputbox-v2", function () {
                        $(this).removeClass('hilight');
                    }).on("keyup", ".inputbox-v2 input", function () {
                        $("#webchannel-email-wrapper, #webchannel-email").removeClass('validation-failed');
                        $(this).attr("value", $(this).val());
                    }).on("click", "#webchannel-submit", function () {
                        $("#webchannel-form").submit();
                    }).on("click", "#optin", function () {
                        $("#optin-wrapper").removeClass('optin-failed');
                    });
                    
                });
            </script>
